2025-02-21T19:32:03Z #11 172.2 To enable CUDA support, UCX requires the CUDA Runtime library (libcudart).
2025-02-21T19:32:03Z #11 172.2 The library can be installed with the appropriate command below:
2025-02-21T19:32:03Z #11 172.2 
2025-02-21T19:32:03Z #11 172.2 * For CUDA 11, run:    conda install cudatoolkit cuda-version=11
2025-02-21T19:32:04Z #11 172.2 * For CUDA 12, run:    conda install cuda-cudart cuda-version=12
2025-02-21T19:32:04Z #11 172.2 
2025-02-21T19:32:04Z #11 172.2 
2025-02-21T19:32:04Z #11 172.2 To enable CUDA support, please follow UCX's instruction above.
2025-02-21T19:32:04Z #11 172.2 
2025-02-21T19:32:04Z #11 172.2 To additionally enable NCCL support, run:    conda install nccl
2025-02-21T19:32:04Z #11 172.2 
2025-02-21T19:32:04Z #11 172.2 
2025-02-21T19:32:04Z #11 172.2 On Linux, Open MPI is built with CUDA awareness but it is disabled by default.
2025-02-21T19:32:04Z #11 172.2 To enable it, please set the environment variable
2025-02-21T19:32:04Z #11 172.2 OMPI_MCA_opal_cuda_support=true
2025-02-21T19:32:04Z #11 172.2 before launching your MPI processes.
2025-02-21T19:32:04Z #11 172.2 Equivalently, you can set the MCA parameter in the command line:
2025-02-21T19:32:04Z #11 172.2 mpiexec --mca opal_cuda_support 1 ...
2025-02-21T19:32:04Z #11 172.2 Note that you might also need to set UCX_MEMTYPE_CACHE=n for CUDA awareness via
2025-02-21T19:32:04Z #11 172.2 UCX. Please consult UCX documentation for further details.
